  <script type="application/javascript">
   var COS_IP = '';
  var COS_COUNTRY = '';
  var COS_CITY = '';
  var COS_REGION = '';
  var COS_LATITUDE = '';
  var COS_LONGITUDE = '';

  function geoip(json){
    COS_IP = json.ip;
    COS_COUNTRY = json.country;
    COS_CITY = json.city;
    COS_REGION = json.region;
    COS_LATITUDE = json.latitude;
    COS_LONGITUDE = json.longitude;
  }
  </script>

    <section class="module span-2 album-reviews-module">
     <h2 class="heading">
      <span>
       <a href="https://consequenceofsound.net/category/cos-exclusive-features/">
        Featured Stories
       </a>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <article class="first">

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function sticky_relocate() {
    if (!jQuery('#sticky-anchor').length) return; 

    var window_top = jQuery(window).scrollTop();
    /*
    if(jQuery("#footermore").length){
            var footer_top = jQuery("#footermore").offset().top;
        }else{
    */
			if(jQuery("#footer").length){
            var footer_top = jQuery("#footer").offset().top;
        	}
    /*
		}
    */
   
    var div_top = jQuery('#sticky-anchor').offset().top;
    var div_height = 350;
    var padding = 20;  
    var win_div = window_top + div_height;
    var footer_top_round = Math.round(footer_top);
    if (win_div > footer_top_round){
        jQuery('#sticky').removeClass('stick');
        jQuery('#sticky').css({bottom: (window_top + div_height - footer_top_round + padding) * -1})
    }else if (window_top > div_top) {
        jQuery('#sticky').addClass('stick');
        jQuery('#sticky').css({bottom: 5});
    } else {
        jQuery('#sticky').removeClass('stick');
    }
}
jQuery(document).ready(function() { 
     if (jQuery('#sticky-anchor').length) {
        jQuery(window).scroll(sticky_relocate);
        sticky_relocate();
    }
});
  </script>

function acEnableTracking() {
    var expiration = new Date(new Date().getTime() + 1000 * 60 * 60 * 24 * 30);
    document.cookie = "ac_enable_tracking=1; expires= " + expiration + "; path=/";
    acTrackVisit();
}

function acTrackVisit() {
    var trackcmp_email = '';
    var trackcmp = document.createElement("script");
    trackcmp.async = true;
    trackcmp.type = 'text/javascript';
    trackcmp.src = '//trackcmp.net/visit?actid=798778651&e='+encodeURIComponent(trackcmp_email)+'&r='+encodeURIComponent(document.referrer)+'&u='+encodeURIComponent(window.location.href);

        trackcmp_h.length && trackcmp_h[0].appendChild(trackcmp);

}
